This slight reduction is expected to attract more consumers, especially given the aggressive growth strategy, while also positioning B02 as a more appealing option compared to competitors.

```
EXPECTED: I anticipate capturing around 10% market share this round, leading to an increase in profit to approximately $1.5 million as we balance the trade-off between volume and margin more effectively.
```

#### Decision Summary:
##### Self-Evaluation of Previous Round:
- **Evaluation:** My predictions for market share and profit were overly optimistic, as I did not capture any market share despite a competitive rate. The decision to set the rate at 450 bps did not resonate with consumers, likely due to the lack of established brand presence and image in a competitive market. Additionally, my execution speed is high, but it wasn't leveraged effectively to draw in customers.
- **Score:** 4/10

- **Rate Set:** 430 bps

```
Round 1:
  • Rate Set: 500 bps
  • Reasoning: Setting the interest rate at 500 bps aligns with the average market rate and positions us competitively in a maintain strategy without undercutting our margins excessively. This rate balances the need to attract a fair share of consumers while maintaining a sustainable profit margin given our cost structure. By not deviating too far from the market average, we also preserve our image score and execution speed in the eyes of consumers.
```
```
  • Expected Outcome: I expect to maintain our market share around 10%, with a potential to capture a few additional loans if our execution speed and image are perceived favorably. Given the loan size and our operating costs, this should allow for a modest profit while ensuring equity remains stable.
```
```
  • Self-Evaluation (Next Round): My previous decision to set the interest rate at 500 bps did not yield the expected market share, as we maintained a 0.0% share despite aiming for around 10%. This indicates that either the rate was too high compared to competitors or our execution speed and image score did not resonate with consumers as anticipated. Overall, the decision was not effective in capturing loans, and we need to adjust our approach.
  • Self-Score: 4/10

Round 2:
```
```
  • Rate Set: 475 bps
  • Reasoning: By lowering the interest rate to 475 bps, I aim to align more closely with the average market rate and potentially attract borrowers who are sensitive to interest rates. This adjustment should enhance our competitiveness and help build our market share, while still allowing us to maintain a reasonable profit margin given our cost structure.
  • Expected Outcome: I anticipate capturing around 5-10% of the market share this round, leading to an increase in profit, potentially exceeding $3 million, as we attract more customers with a more appealing rate.
```
```
  • Self-Evaluation (Next Round): My prediction of capturing 5-10% market share with a rate of 475 bps was somewhat accurate, as we maintained a 7.1% market share, leading to a profit of $2,737,800. However, while the profit was as expected, it fell short of the higher potential I anticipated. Overall, the decision allowed us to stay competitive; however, I underestimated the need for a more aggressive rate reduction to significantly increase our market presence.
```
